List the id and the maker . SQl: select t1.id ,  t1.maker from car_makers as t1 join model_list as t2 on t1.id  =  t2.maker group by t1.id having count(*)  >=  2 intersect select t1.id ,  t1.maker from car_makers as t1 join model_list as t2 on t1.id  =  t2.maker join car_names as t3 on t2.model  =  t3.model group by t1.id having count(*)  >  3; ###
